mirvaso contains the active substance brimonidine , which belongs to a group of medicines called alpha agonists . it is used to treat the skin on the face to reduce redness and rosacea . rosacemia is a condition where high levels of blood flow in the facial skin are caused by enlargement ( dilation ) of the small blood vessels of the skin . mirvasa acts by reducing the size of the blood vessels and reducing their ability to carry excess blood flow . this reduces redness .

kinzalmono belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . angiostensin is a substance produced by the body , which causes blood vessels to narrow , causing your blood pressure to rise . kinzulmono blocks the activity of angiodensin in the body and helps the blood vessels relax , thus lowering your bloodpressure . this helps your blood vessels recover and your blood flow is controlled . the high blood pressure is caused by the high pressure . high bloodpressure can damage blood vessels in several organs , leading to heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness .
